Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-401 Penalty for violation.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-401(1): Title 63G, Chapter 4, Administrative Procedures Act If an owner-operator or operator violates a provision of this chapter with respect to an amusement ride, in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-401(1)(a): deny, suspend, or revoke, in whole or in part, the owner-operator's annual amusement ride permit or multi-ride permit for the amusement ride; or
Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-401(1)(b): impose fines or administrative penalties in accordance with rules made by the committee.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-401(2): Upon a violation of a provision of this chapter, the director may file an action in district court to enjoin the operation of an amusement ride.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-16-402 Audit -- Right of entry.
--------------------------------------------------------
The director or the director's representative, upon presenting appropriate credentials to the owner-operator, operator, or agent in charge, may enter a premises where an amusement ride is located for the purpose of auditing compliance with the provisions of this chapter.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 72 - Chapter 17 - Rail Safety
*********************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101 Office of Rail Safety -- Creation -- Applicability.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(1): In accordance with 49 C.F.R.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(2): As described in 49 C.F.R. Secs. 212.105 and 212.107, to organize the Office of Rail Safety, the executive director shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(2)(a): enter into an agreement with the Federal Railroad Administration to participate in inspection and investigation activities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(2)(b): obtain certification from the Federal Railroad Administration to undertake inspection and investigative responsibilities and duties.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(3): In establishing the Office of Rail Safety in accordance with the duties described in 49 C.F.R.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(4): This chapter applies to:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(4)(a): a class I railroad; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-101(4)(b): commuter rail.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102(1): "Class I railroad" means the same as that term is defined in 49 U.S.C. Sec. 20102.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102(2): 63N-3-602 "Commuter rail" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102(3): "Federal Railroad Administration" means the Federal Railroad Administration created in 49 U.S.C. Sec. 103.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102(4): 72-17-101 "Office" means the Office of Rail Safety created in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-102(5): "Railroad" means the same as that term is defined in 49 C.F.R. Sec. 200.3.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103 Duties of the Office of Rail Safety.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1): In accordance with 49 C.F.R.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(a): grade crossings;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(b): hazardous materials;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(c): motive power and equipment;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(d): operating practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(e): signal and train control; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(1)(f): track.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(2): (1) As part of the responsibilities described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(2)(a): inspect and investigate railroad rights-of-way, facilities, equipment, and operations of railroads in this state;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(2)(b): notify a railroad of any violation or lack of compliance with applicable state and federal laws, rules, regulations, orders, and directives;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(2)(c): enforce applicable state and federal laws, rules, regulations, orders, and directives relating to the transportation by rail of persons or commodities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(2)(d): issue orders to require compliance with state and federal laws, rules, regulations, orders, and directives.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(3): The office shall employ a sufficient number of federally certified inspectors and staff to ensure that railroad equipment, facilities, and tracks are inspected as frequently as reasonably required to ensure compliance and safety as required under state and federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(a): The office shall investigate railroad practices related to the length of time a railroad blocks a highway-railroad grade crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(b): Upon petition of a political subdivision, or upon the office's own motion, the office may:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(b)(i): conduct an investigation of the conditions related to a grade crossing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(b)(ii): if necessary, conduct a hearing, make findings, and issue an order to determine whether highway-railroad crossing blocking practices of the railroad are reasonable.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c)(i): The office shall examine and inspect the physical condition of all railroad facilities in this state to ensure compliance with safety requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c)(ii): As part of the inspection and examination of railroad facilities and crossings, the office shall include an examination and inspection of:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c)(ii)(A): the condition of railroad facilities and crossing infrastructure;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c)(ii)(B): whether expansion of grade crossing infrastructure or other changes are justified based on the traffic and safety conditions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(c)(ii)(C): other safety considerations required by federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(d): If the office determines that a railroad's highway-railroad crossing blocking practices are unreasonable, the office shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(d)(i): request the Federal Railroad Administration take enforcement actions pursuant to 49 C.F.R. Sec. 212.115; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(d)(ii): notify the Surface Transportation Board defined in 49 U.S.C. Sec. 10102 of the unsafe and unreasonable practices.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(4)(e): If the office finds a violation of safety requirements as described in this section or in federal law, and the office requests an enforcement action and Federal Railroad Administration does not take enforcement action as described in 49 C.F.R. Sec. 212.115, the office may seek a civil penalty not less than $500 and no more than $10,000 for each offense.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5): (5)(b); (5)(d); (5)(e); (5)(d); (6); 72-17-107
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(a): The office shall examine and inspect the physical condition of all railroad facilities in this state to ensure compliance with safety requirements.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(b): If an inspector determines that a railroad facility is noncompliant, the office shall provide written notice to the railroad.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(c): (5)(b) If a railroad receives a notice described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(d): If after 30 days from the date of the notice the railroad has not remedied the condition or practice to the office's satisfaction, the office may set the matter for hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(e): (5)(d) After a hearing described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(e)(i): eliminate or remedy the unsafe or unlawful condition or practice; or
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(e)(ii): make any necessary repairs, alterations, or other changes to the relevant condition or practice to ensure compliance with state and federal law.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(f): (5)(e); (5)(d); (6); 72-17-107 In addition to any order issued under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(f)(i): after 48 hours' written notice to the railroad, issue an order prohibiting:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(f)(i)(A): the unsafe or unlawful practice; or
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(f)(i)(B): the use of the facility until completion of the necessary repair, alteration, or other necessary changes; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(5)(f)(ii): (6); 72-17-107 pay a civil penalty of not more than $10,000 per violation or per day of violation of state or federal law, or a rule made in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(6): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act In accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(6)(a): establish the Office of Rail Safety as required in this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(6)(b): establish and enforce rules regarding safe and reasonable procedures and standards regarding the blocking of grade crossings, which standards and limits shall be commensurate with reasonable requirements of train and vehicular traffic operations;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(6)(c): enforce this part and relevant state and federal law related to this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-103(6)(d): administer the Office of Rail Safety as described in this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106 Office of Rail Safety Account.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(1): There is created an expendable special revenue fund called the Office of Rail Safety Account.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(2): 72-17-105 The account shall be funded by:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(2)(a): deposits into the account by the Legislature;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(2)(b): 72-17-105 fees collected pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(2)(c): other deposits or donations into the account.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(3): (3)(a); (c) The office shall provide a detailed budget to account for the office's expenditures related to the enforcement of this part, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(3)(a): salaries, per diem, and travel expenses of employees performing the duties described in this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(3)(b): expenditures for clerical and support staff directly associated with the duties described in this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(3)(c): expenditures for legal staff who pursue and administer complaints and compliance issues related to this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(3)(d): (3)(a); (c) reasonable overhead costs related to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(4): The office, in performing the duties under this part:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(4)(a): shall limit the expenditure of funds to the total amount of fees collected from the railroads as described in this section; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-106(4)(b): may not expend funds from other sources accessible to the department.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107 Rulemaking regarding railroad clearances and walkways.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
In accordance withUtah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(1): walkways adjacent to railroad track;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(2): clearances of structures and other obstructions near railroad track;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(3): the safety of office personnel conducting inspections in accordance with this part;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(4): railroad infrastructure and work spaces for railroad workers;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(5): signage related to railroad worker safety; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-107(6): other safety standards as the department finds necessary.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108 Agreements to indemnify in a railroad contract.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(a): "Railroad contract" means a contract or agreement between:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(a)(i): a railroad; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(a)(ii): another person that could be subject to a civil penalty or fine issued pursuant to this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(b): "Indemnification provision" means a covenant, promise, agreement, or understanding in, in connection with, or collateral to a railroad contract that requires the person to insure, hold harmless, indemnify, or defend the railroad against liability, if:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(b)(i): the damages arise out of a civil penalty issued pursuant to this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(1)(b)(ii): the damages are caused by or resulting from the fault of the railroad or the railroad's agents or employees.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(2): (3) Except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(3): (1)(b)(i) If an indemnification provision is included in a railroad contract, in any action for damages described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(3)(a): the damages are caused in part by the party other than the railroad;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(3)(b): the cause of the damages arose at a time when the party other than the railroad was operating pursuant to the railroad contract.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-108(4): This section may not be construed to impair a contract in existence before May 3, 2023.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201(1): "Highway-railroad grade crossing" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201(1)(a): an intersection where a railroad track crosses a highway at the same level; or
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201(1)(b): an intersection where the railroad track of a railroad entity crosses the railroad track of another railroad entity at the same level.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201(2): 54-1-1 "Public Service Commission" means the Public Service Commission of Utah created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-201(3): "Railroad entity" means an entity, a company, a person, or a public transit provider that owns, controls, operates, or manages a railroad.


Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202 Regulation of highway-railroad grade crossings.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(1): A railroad entity may not construct a new highway-railroad grade crossing without first obtaining written authorization from the department.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2): (4) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(a): determine and prescribe:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(a)(i): the specific location of each highway-railroad grade crossing in the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(a)(ii): the terms of installation, operation, maintenance, use, and protection of each highway-railroad grade crossing in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(b): alter or abolish any highway-railroad grade crossing upon such terms and conditions as the department prescribes;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(c): restrict the use of any highway-railroad grade crossing to certain types of traffic in the interest of public safety;
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(d): when practicable, as determined by the department, require a separation of grades at any existing highway-railroad grade crossing in the state, and prescribe the terms of any separation of grades at an existing highway-railroad grade crossing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(2)(e): allocate responsibilities, including costs, for the alteration, abolition, or separation of any highway-railroad grade crossing in the state between each affected railroad entity and highway authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(a): The department shall allocate maintenance responsibilities, including costs, for each highway-railroad grade crossing in the state, including the maintenance of related safety devices and crossing materials, between each railroad entity and highway authority affected by the highway-railroad grade crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(b): The department may base the allocation of maintenance responsibilities, including costs, on ownership and control of the right-of-way, crossing materials, signals and devices, or other factors the department determines are appropriate to protect public safety.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(c): If a railroad entity or a highway authority disagrees with the department's allocation of maintenance responsibilities, including costs, for a specific highway-railroad grade crossing:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(c)(i): the railroad entity or highway authority may provide a written request to the department for a review of the allocation describing reasons for modification of the allocation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(c)(ii): the department:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(c)(ii)(A): shall conduct a review of the allocation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(c)(ii)(B): at the department's discretion, may modify the allocation.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(d): Unless the department provides prior written approval, responsibility for the costs of maintenance at a highway-railroad grade crossing as allocated by the department may not be modified or waived by agreement between a railroad entity and a local highway authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(3)(e): Unless the department enters into a written agreement with a railroad entity stating otherwise, the relevant railroad entity is responsible for using railroad employees to perform the physical maintenance and labor at a highway-railroad grade crossing and shall comply with Code of Federal Regulations, Title 49, Transportation.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4): 54-7-25
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4)(a): The department may require or authorize the construction of a new highway-railroad grade crossing or the improvement of an existing highway-railroad grade crossing if:
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4)(a)(i): the new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing is to be funded solely by non-federal funds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4)(a)(ii): the department determines, after consultation with any affected railroad entities and highway authorities, that the new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing will improve the safety of the public in accordance with requirements established by the department to determine the need, design, and impacts of the new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4)(b): The railroad entity affected by the new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing shall timely enter into a written agreement with the department regarding the design and installation of the new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(4)(c): 54-7-25 If a railroad entity does not make reasonable efforts to participate in determining the need, design, and impacts of a new or improved crossing, does not timely enter into an agreement with the department, or fails to timely provide a design and install improvements as described in an agreement, the department may impose and the railroad shall pay a penalty consistent with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(5): A railroad entity affected by a new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing may not require up-front payment of costs as a condition for the railroad entity's review, approval, or inspection of a new or improved highway-railroad grade crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(6): If the department determines that public convenience and necessity demand the establishment, creation, or construction of a crossing of a street or highway over, under, or upon the tracks or lines of any public utility, the department may by order, decision, rule, or decree require the establishment, construction, or creation of such crossing, and such crossing shall thereupon become a public highway and crossing.
Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(7): (7)(b); 19-3-318; (7)(a); 54-7-24; 54-7-21

Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(7)(b): 19-3-318; (7)(a) If a petition is filed by a person or entity engaged in a subject activity, as defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 72-17-202(7)(c)(i): 54-7-24 direct commencement of an action as provided for in Section
